<Text>Instagram: @koganei037

1st Impression:
From the outside it looks like it got a lot of space but once you go in, you realize that the space is only long but not far in. Making larger groups hard to be seated.
Other than that, the bar area and overall ambiance is nice and clean.

Food Impression:
The Pan Roast here is ok but I've had better in other places.
This one still cannot compare to the Oyster Bar located inside Palace Station in Las Vegas.
The heat numbering is a joke. I ordered a 7 while a friend of mine ordered a 8 (1 to 10), we both barely got any heat on our Pan Roasts and Gumbo.

Price Impression:
The price is about the same with other places that serves the same type of food but because of the lack of quality, it's just ok.

Conclusion:
Better save your money and try somewhere else than here. The cost is not worth trying an ok place for Pan Roast.<//Text><Rating>3<//Rating><Gmap_id>0x80dd2143cf92ab6b:0xd7bc543c8625f45a< /Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>
<userid>102918253898437847981<//userid>< name>
Rodney S</name>
< time>
1526354306354<//time>
<rating>4< /rating>< text>
Ritter me this, Batman!

What do you get when you cross an owl with a bungee cord??

............................My ass!! BWAHAHAHAHAHAHAHA

Free appetizer with any entr√©e purchase coupon

Ritter's Steam Kettle Cooking serves up authentic Creole cuisine, utilizing individual jacketed steam kettles to evenly cook food at varying temperatures.  I've had this place on my radar for awhile now, and lunch seemed the perfect opportunity to stop by.

While the restaurant seems small, the table & bar seating can accommodate around 30 people.  Flatscreen TV's had international soccer & soap operas for my viewing pleasure.

A complimentary crusty bread roll w/ butter greeted me as I gave the menu a once over.

For my free appetizer, I went with the deep fried bacon wrapped molasses marinated shrimp & mozzarella with molasses mustard-
Bacon & shrimp, two of my favorite food groups.  Large, tender shrimp wrapped in smoky, fatty bacon, with a delicious mustard for dipping.  If that's not enough, gooey mozzarella cheese just for the hell of it.  Some hot sauce kicked up the molasses mustard to my liking.

For my entr√©e, I chose the clam pan roast (spice level 7)-
Tomato cream base with Cajun trinity & jasmine rice.  A rainy day comfort food.  Rich, hearty, stick to your ribs kind of dish.  The level 7 spice level was just right for me, providing heat while still allowing me to taste all the bold flavors encompassed in the bowl.  Plenty of sweet clam swimming in the tomato broth, a scoop of fluffy rice wading in the middle.  My only complaint, and it's more a personal preference, is next time I'll ask for rice on the side.  Reason being is that I'm not particularly fond of soggy rice.  As I got down to the last few bites, the soggy rice grains became unappetizing to me.  But, the large portions & tremendous flavor have made me a fan.

Beignet with chocolate whipped cream-
I've only had beignets previously at Ralph Brennan's Jazz Kitchen, and Ritter's seemed more dense & textured.  The chocolate whipped cream was ambrosia to me.  With a liberal slathering on top of the fried dough calorie buster, the flavor was heavenly.  Perfect way to end the meal.

Service was great.  I was attended to promptly & had plenty of soda water w/lime refills.  Parking is metered in the front, with a structure available nearby.  The parking structure is only $2 for the first two hours.

C'est si bon!  Ritter's Steam Kettle Cooking offers delicious Creole cuisine in a relaxing atmosphere.  I'm highly anticipating coming back & trying their other dishes such as jambalaya & chowder.  Besides beignets, Ritter's also offers bread pudding a la mode and that has my undivided attention for my next visit.

Highly recommend!
NOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOMNOM< /text>

One of the more unique food experiences you can get in downtown Huntington Beach. It is sort quaint (small) but one of the few places with counter service where lone diners can eat without taking up a table and stares of other patrons. The service was very attentive and helpful. I had the pan toast and had the chowder before and intend to get the gumbo in the future. < review>
I had the Cajun Calamari and the New England clam chowder bowl which were both very good and came in a good enough portion to share with another person. I also had the Diablo shrimp pasta bowl which was also big enough to share. It had 6 medium shrimp, about a 20 count/lb size and I had it at an 8/10 heat level. The prawns were a good texture, not overcooked and the heat level was nice and not overpowering. I will say that they red sauce was very basic and left me wanting something more complex but that's not to say it wasn't good just not great. I finished up with some beignets for dessert which were made great, fluffy and crispy on the outside but still slightly doughy and soft on the inside with a pocket of air.  These were served with plenty of powdered sugar and a light chocolate mousse which topped them nicely.<//review>

I've passed by this restaurant this many times and never knew that it served Cajun food. I love Cajun food so when I found out, I just had to try it.

I got the jambalaya and my friend got the gumbo.the food came our surprisingly quick for Cajun cuisine and I was a little wary, but it was all for naught.

<Rating>4</Rating>< review>
Pretty good place for a southern taste.

The restaurant is a bit small, holding maybe 40 people at most. It's a cozy place though. They have nice decor and have their cooking stream pots lined up along the bar. It actually gets kinda hot sitting at the bar when they cook.

The food was good. We had their oysters and their house pot roast. I felt that the oysters were fresh. The pot roast was good as well. The amount of lobster and shrimp was substantial and it tastes overall very good.

Overall, it is a bit pricey but it may become my goto place for oysters.</review>

< Review>
My boyfriend and I stayed here for our trip out to LA and we couldn't have chosen a better place to stay. We stayed in the Abbot Kinney Suite, and it was a great experience. The suite had an open separate bedroom with desk and dresser with night tables on each side and a living room with a fire place. There was a cute kitchen with a deep sink and a claw foot tub and nicely tiled bathroom. The suite had windows everywhere and had massive amounts of sunlight. When you stepped out there was a balcony that overlooked Rose Ave and Venice Beach. (BEAUTIFUL) We sat our there often drinking and enjoying the view and atmosphere of Venice. The staff and owner were super nice and accommodating. The street was semi busy during the day and quite at night. There is a lot of restaurants around and the boardwalk is only steps away. The street parking was great. We always found a spot in front of the hotel. We came there to visit all of LA but just ended up stay in the area and keeping The Rose as our home base. Totally recommend staying here if you want to be away from all the crazy of the city and live like a local.< /Review>

< Review>
Bunched little stuff.  No night manger if the is a problem, even though the State requires a night manager if you have 11+ rooms.  There is no hotel parking, so If you are unlucky enough to not find street parking, you are stuck with a $30-45/night parking tab - which is what happens in the summer and weekends. they tell you they have a deal with the parking lot across the street, but you can cut a deal with them for $30/day.  The 'hotel deal' is $15 day+ $27.50/night.  Best to negotiate your own deal with the adjacent parking lots.

The basic rooms are really small, with a sink and the toilet/showers are down the hall.  Within my comfort zone, but not most women.  The soap/shampoo dispenser had fallen off the wall and it was interesting juggling a 3-soap dispenser while showering.

The hotel is 20 yards from central Venice Beach, so be ready for noise.  Although the they supply earplugs.

It is very clean, the staff is nice, but they have many managerial  items to figure out.

A bit more work and experience and I am sure they will bump to 3+ in a year or so.<//Review>

< text>
One of my favorite Asian dessert places in the city offering a large variety of sweet vs savory light bites and Chinese desserts. What's great is they are open late and the price is right. Whenever I go there it's almost always packed and the service really isn't great.

We have tried a number of things on the menu and you really cannot go wrong. The past visit we got these curry balls which were ok, ramen, basil popcorn chicken and mango slush with sago and fresh fruit. Everything was really tasty and the popcorn chicken went really well with the curry sauce. We inhaled it. So good.

When in the city, we must always go here to try.< /text>

< Review>
A local boba tea establishment in my neighborhood also has lots of other kinds of sweet treats and goodies. I had the coconut milk which was completely delicious; really strong coconut taste with icy slush to complement it. My wife had the green tea ice cream which was also very good. Usually this place is packed with lots of schoolkids from the area. On this day they were not as busy so we were afforded much time to enjoy the ambiance. They also offered us hot tea in addition to what we ordered. Will definitely go back for the coconut milk if not something else on the menu.<//Review>

< text>
Great little Asian dessert place with many choices of sago and fruit. I come here with my friends during late nights when I am around the Sunset. I enjoy the tea and the quick service by their workers. The staff are friendly and attentive to customers. The place is usually filled on the weekends, so be prepared to wait a few minutes to get a table and the place is cash only.< /text>

Jessica Gong< /name>
<Text>Try the watermelon sago! It's very refreshing and delicious. They load tons of fruit into it so your are for sure getting your five-a-day no doubt about it.

If fruit sago isn't your thing, they have tons of other sago and sweet desserts that are a must try. It reminds me Hong Kong and eating at all the dessert shops.

The servings are so big that I don't finish most of the time. You never have to worry about them ripping you off with teeny tiny serving sizes.

The waitress is really nice. The moment you sit down she brings over cups of hot all for your whole party before you even say anything to her. Love it!<//Text></record>

<Text>Customer service was not their best quality here by the way. We seated ourselves and waited a while to order, get our food, and check out. Parking can be difficult to find here as well.

The restaurant was a little small. I would estimate that the maximum capacity was 20 people.

In regards to their food, I would say it's average. You get what you pay for. I got the coconut milk with grass jelly (I believe) and it was recently sweet. Not over the top which was a good midnight snack. We also got popcorn chicken. It was nothing special and had to season it with this spicy Japanese powder.

Would I come back here? Yeah I would. The food here is affordable.<//Text>< gmapID>

< Review>
If you want results and you enjoy work outs that are the perfect level of challenging at whatever skill level you are, go to The Camp! My husband did the 20 lb challenge twice and took me to their Pack the Camp day and I loved it! I decided to join for 4 months after 2 months of giving birth and at the end of my membership I weighed less than my pre-pregnancy weight. The trainers are awesome and they do a fantastic job motivating you, not to mention everyone is very friendly and inviting.

For those concerned about the price, I thought it was a pricy membership but when I went to other local specialty gyms, such as Orange Theory and pilates, The Camp turned out to be cheaper because you can go to all the classes every day for their base price (1 gym location). At the other places you would pay up to $80-$100 more for that same unlimited privilege.< /Review>

I came here because reviews were saying they had good portions and good pricing. However, I was a bit disappointed when I got my meal.

I ordered one Beef Udon and my husband ordered the Joe's Roll. The udon was not a traditional Japanese udon and the beef was more like potroast.

The roll was really small, especially for the price. The tables were sticky and the atmosphere was really awkward and claustrophobic. In addition, they don't follow COVID seating regulations.

The older man (who I assume runs the restaurant) was really rude to my friend. My friend tried to order a kid's meal and the older man kind of scolded him, saying it was for 9 and under. However, the age limit wasn't stated on the menu.

The younger waitors are nice, but that's not enough of a reason for me to return.<//Text>

<UserId.>112265102739780182237<//UserId.>< review>
My co-worker and I found this place when we were going to the Thai place next door. We noticed the Pho shop and decided to give it a try, since it was a new restaurant for us and we both enjoy Pho.

The interior was casual, but not sloppy.  Very clean with a relaxed atmosphere.  The staff was helpful and always had a smile.

The Pho was very good, and the veggie plate was fresh and crisp.  The broth used was outstanding and the meat in my bowl was extremely tender and tasty.  I don't always find the meat in a bowl of Pho to be all that tasty at most Pho restaurants (maybe it's the way they cook the meat; maybe it's the fact that the meat has been boiling too long and has released all its flavor).

This Pho restaurant was an exception, as the meats were tender and flavorful.

My co-worker and I will definitely be back, as we have added this restaurant to our short-list of places to dine while in the Mountain View/Sunnyvale area.

The only reason I didn't give Luv Pho 5 full stars is that they do not offer a B√°nh m√¨ Sandwich, which is a wonderful sandwich to experience if you haven't.  Add some B√°nh m√¨ sandwiches to the menu and this would be the perfect Pho hot spot.<//review>

< Review>
I recently had McCarthy Painting & Finishing paint the exterior of my home and one interior room. The crew was prompt, courteous and left the workplace each day in a neat and clean state.

The quality of the exterior job was fantastic and the crew regularly communicated about any questions or issues that developed.  Definitely a 5-star job. The place looks great!

The interior room proved a bit problematic as we were covering a dark color with white. After multiple coats I was informed that there would be an additional charge to continue and cover the remaining bleed-through. Brendan was professional and courteous and we negotiated a reasonable extra charge for the additional materials and time. I greatly appreciate his balancing the need to make a reasonable profit with holding to the original contract and meeting my expectations. So despite the technical issues, I am quite satisfied and also consider the interior job to be a 5-star rating.

I would definitely have McCarthy back for any additional painting needs.<//Review>

Beautiful park grounds to walk around, just watch out for the flying frisbees. This park features a very large frisbee golf course - I didn't even know that was a thing outside of Golf Story. The course is laid out amongst beautiful trees, along a creek, and setup around some fields. You are welcome to walk through the area, just be aware of very fast-moving frisbees flying around. There is also 2 playgrounds, including one for toddlers. But the star of this park is the frisbee course.</Review>
